store_key = 'cfg/name', param_key = 'name', param_type = 'string'
value = 'store-name', version = 2, default = 'fallback'

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        ("store_key", "param_key", "param_type", "value", "version", "default"),
        [
            ("cfg/name", "name", "string", "store-name", 2, "fallback"),
            ("config/port-number", "api_port", "integer", "8088", 3, None),
            ("cfg/name", "name", "string", "", 1, "fallback"),
            ("cfg/port", "port", "integer", "9001", 0, None),
            ("cfg/feature flag&name", "feature_name", "string", "enabled", 2, None),
        ],
        ids=[
            "default-fallback",
            "key-mismatch",
            "empty-string",
            "version-zero",
            "url-encoded",
        ],
    )
    def test_primary_store_resolves(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        store_server,
        store_key: str,
        param_key: str,
        param_type: str,
        value: str,
        version: int,
        default: str | None,
    ) -> None:
        """Primary-store lookup across variants."""
        store_server.set_primary(store_key, value, version=version)
        field: dict[str, object] = {"type": param_type, "primary-store": store_key}
        if default is not None:
            field["default"] = default
        schema_path = _write_schema(tmp_path, {param_key: field})
    
        result = run_cfgpipe(
            entrypoint_argv,
            schema_path=schema_path,
            global_args=["--primary-store", store_server.address],
            cwd=tmp_path,
        )
    
>       assert_success(result)

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f19f0fc80>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f18983a10>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f185f8b00>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

.evaluation_tests/utils.py:216:

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f186ae060>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f1852dee0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f19390e00>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f18983a10>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

.evaluation_tests/utils.py:216: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f184a0b60>, block = True, timeout = 1.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f18392720>, block = True, timeout = 1.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x7a5f183176b0>, block = True, timeout = 1.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty
